‚óŹ¬†User answered Claude's questions:
  ‚éŅ ¬†¬∑ Generalizing to named phases: should the existing 'check' hook name be 
     renamed to 'site_pre' outright, or kept as a working alias? A clean rename 
     touches check/umich/__init__.py (2 registrations), conftest.py's reset_sc 
     fixture, and 4 test files ‚ÄĒ all in-repo, no external consumers I can find. 
     An alias keeps old registrations working but adds permanent indirection to 
     the brand-new phase registry. ‚Üí Clean rename (Recommended)
     ¬∑ Where exactly should site_post_dns fire? The natural spot per your PROMPT
     is right after custom_domains/primary_domain are computed (~line 1700) ‚ÄĒ 
     but the existing DNS/Cloudflare notice blocks (not-behind-cloudflare, 
     not-proxied, multi-zone, not-in-dns; lines ~1806-1918) and the 
     site_url/WordPress-network detection (a wp_eval call, ~1783) come after 
     that point. Firing at ~1700 means cache-check warnings are inserted before 
     those existing warnings (within the warning group of the report), and the 
     phase contract stays clean (no WP data yet). Firing after ~1918 keeps 
     existing notice order but puts a WP gather call before a phase named 
     'post_dns'. ‚Üí After domain loop ~1700 (Recommended)
     ¬∑ What should [Cloudflare.cachecheck].enabled default to when the key (or 
     whole subsection) is absent? Context: when enabled, the egress-IP test 
     requires account_id + list_name config (fatal if missing, per 
     zero-silent-failures) ‚ÄĒ so 'default true' means any existing adopter with 
     [Cloudflare].enabled=true who upgrades gets a fatal error until they add 
     list config or set enabled=false. 'Default false' means U-M must explicitly
     flip it on in the live config as part of rollout, and a future adopter 
     could silently never get the check. ‚Üí Default false, opt-in (Recommended)
     ¬∑ Dual-stack hosts create an egress-IP blind spot: the trace to 
     https://1.1.1.1 (IPv4 literal) verifies your IPv4 egress address, but httpx
     requests to site FQDNs may go over IPv6 (or vice versa) ‚ÄĒ so the verified 
     address may not be the address the actual cache-test requests come from, 
     defeating the allowlist check's purpose (ensuring requests aren't 
     challenged/treated as external). How should we close this? ‚Üí Verify both 
     families

‚óŹ¬†User answered Claude's questions:
  ‚éŅ ¬†¬∑ Redirect budget: the PROMPT says "replace the initial URL with the new 
     one and re-request a maximum of 5 times per original FQDN". Two readings: 
     (a) each requested URL gets its own chain of up to 5 same-FQDN redirects 
     before we give up on that URL; (b) one shared budget of 5 redirect-follows 
     across ALL URLs tested for that FQDN (main page + 3 links + assets 
     combined) ‚ÄĒ once spent, any further redirect ends that URL's consideration.
     Which did you intend? ‚Üí Per-URL chain, max 5 (Recommended)
     ¬∑ How should the new check be covered at the e2e/golden tier? The terminus 
     shim doesn't intercept HTTP, and goldens run as a subprocess 
     (monkeypatching doesn't reach it). Today all golden configs have 
     [Cloudflare].enabled=false, so goldens are untouched by default. Options 
     for proving the notice HTML renders correctly end-to-end. ‚Üí Integration + 
     render-unit (Recommended)
     ¬∑ The RNG that picks up to 3 links and up to 1 JS/CSS/image asset: tests 
     will seed it, but what about production runs? Unseeded means a re-run picks
     different pages (hard to reproduce a reported problem); seeding from (site
     name + report date) means re-running the same report reproduces identical 
     selections, and selections rotate month to month. ‚Üí Seed site+date 
     (Recommended)
     ¬∑ Response body limits: pages must be downloaded to parse links/assets, but
     a page could be huge, and assets (images, JS) don't need bodies at all ‚ÄĒ 
     only response headers. Impose limits? ‚Üí No limits

‚óŹ¬†User answered Claude's questions:
  ‚éŅ ¬†¬∑ Expansion 1 ‚ÄĒ Relocate the existing fqdns-gated U-M checks now that the 
     seam exists. CLAUDE.md defers moving the umich-cloudflare-plugin / 
     Drupal-module / Hummingbird checks (main script ~lines 1993, 2338) into 
     check/umich because they need a post-gather hook ‚ÄĒ which this task creates 
     (site_post_gather). Doing it now: effort medium (move ~2 blocks + their 
     tests; goldens likely unchanged since they fire only when 
     fqdns_behind_cloudflare is non-empty, which goldens never have); risk is a 
     larger diff in the same change. Deferring: the phase contract ships 
     unproven by a second consumer. ‚Üí Include in scope
     ¬∑ Expansion 2 ‚ÄĒ Extend gate_disabled_sections() to nested tables. Today 
     only top-level [Section] enabled=false strips settings before substitution;
     [Cloudflare.cachecheck] has no secrets so this task doesn't need it, but 
     any future subsection carrying a <{secret ‚Ä¶}> would silently require its 
     secrets even when disabled. Effort: small (recursive walk + tests). Risk: 
     low, but it's speculative generality (YAGNI) until a subsection actually 
     carries secrets. ‚Üí Include in scope
     ¬∑ Expansion 3 ‚ÄĒ MISS‚ÜíHIT cache-behavior verification. Headers can look 
     perfectly cacheable while caching still fails in practice (e.g. a Vary 
     header or cookie interplay). Requesting each URL twice and flagging when 
     the second response isn't HIT/STALE/REVALIDATED would catch that class. 
     Effort: small-medium (doubles request count per site, one new result-item 
     type). Risk: occasional false positives (colo eviction between requests, 
     low-traffic sites) ‚ÄĒ wording would need to hedge; also doubles run time 
     spent in this check. ‚Üí Include this in scope, pause 2 seconds between a 
     MISS and a second request to ensure that Cloudflare has time to actually 
     cache the request (reduce the chance of a false MISS on the second request 
     due to issuing the request too quickly), if it's still a MISS then pause 
     another 2 seconds before making a third (final) attempt. If it's still a 
     MISS after the third attempt, add a result notice explaining the problem 
     and suggested course of action. I acknowledge this change may substantially
     increase the time the program takes to run.
     ¬∑ Expansion 4 ‚ÄĒ Persist cache-check results. Store per-FQDN/per-URL results
     in a DB table each run (like PantheonTraffic) so future runs can trend 
     ("newly broken since last month"), suppress repeat notices, or feed the 
     planned portal integration. Effort: medium (new model, --create-tables 
     addition, retention question). Risk: schema commitment now for a consumer 
     that doesn't exist yet; the notices CSV output already gives a flat-file 
     record per run. ‚Üí NOT in scope

‚óŹ¬†User answered Claude's questions:
  ‚éŅ ¬†¬∑ Scoping the MISS-retry protocol: should the 2s/retry/2s/retry sequence 
     fire on EVERY first-response MISS, or only when the response otherwise 
     looks cacheable (no no-store/private/no-cache, a real max-age/s-maxage ‚Č• 
     the 3-day floor)? If Cache-Control already disqualifies caching, a 
     persistent MISS is expected and already flagged by the Cache-Control result
     items ‚ÄĒ retrying just adds ~4s per URL and a redundant result item. 
     (EXPIRED/STALE/REVALIDATED/UPDATING/HIT would never trigger retries ‚ÄĒ they 
     all prove the object reaches cache.) ‚Üí Only when cacheable (Recommended)
     ¬∑ Expansion 5 ‚ÄĒ a fast single-purpose diagnostic mode. --only-warn runs ALL
     checks including the slow WP/Drush gather. A '--check cloudflare-cache 
     SITE'-style mode (skip traffic DB, skip WP/Drush, run just the DNS/domain 
     classification + this check, console output only) would let you or a site 
     owner-facing consultant diagnose one site in seconds. Effort: small-medium 
     (a new gate in main(); the phase system makes it mostly a matter of which 
     invoke_hooks run). Risk: another CLI path to keep working; scope creep in a
     task that's already grown. ‚Üí NOT in scope
     ¬∑ U-M documentation deliverables in the SPEC: exploration found most of the
     four doc pages have NO heading anchors (only #useragent on the Drupal page
     and '#rule 1'‚Ä¶'#rule 4' on cache-rules ‚ÄĒ ids with literal spaces), so 
     deep-linking from notices is mostly impossible today. How far should the 
     spec's documentation suggestions go? (You said only suggest edits when more
     than trivially beneficial ‚ÄĒ both options below meet that bar in my 
     judgment; the second costs you more manual work.) ‚Üí Also draft new page 
     (Recommended)
     ¬∑ Expansion 6 ‚ÄĒ also test the http‚Üíhttps redirect on each FQDN's main page?
     One extra request per FQDN to http://fqdn/ verifying it redirects to https
     (site owners occasionally break this, leaving http visitors on an insecure
     page that also bypasses some Cloudflare features). Effort: tiny (one 
     request + one result-item type). Risk: marginal scope growth; arguably a 
     security check rather than a cache check (could belong to the future 
     'Cloudflare/security scoring' TODO instead). ‚Üí NOT in scope

  ‚éŅ ¬†Plan saved to: 
     ~/.claude/plans/development-2026-07-08-cloudflare-cache-optimized-cocke.md 
     ¬∑ /plan to edit
     Cloudflare cache-configuration check + named-phase hook system

     Context

     Site owners on Pantheon-behind-Cloudflare frequently misconfigure caching
     (missing/short
     Cache-Control, cookies on public content, BYPASS/DYNAMIC cache statuses),
     losing the cost
     and performance benefits Cloudflare provides. This task adds a
     check/cloudflare/ package that
     probes each proxied FQDN's pages/assets over HTTP and adds actionable
     "Cloudflare caching"
     warning notices to the monthly report. Prerequisite: generalize the
     hardcoded
     setup/check hook pair into an ordered, named, documented phase system so
     this check (and all
     future de-monolith moves) has a seam with the right data available.
     Requirements source:
     development/2026-07-08-cloudflare-cache-configuration/PROMPT.md + an
     extensive interview
     (all decisions below are user-approved and binding).

     Post-approval workflow (per PROMPT.md methodology): on plan approval, (1)
     write
     development/2026-07-08-cloudflare-cache-configuration/SPEC.md from this
     plan, (2) run the
     adversarial review loop (independent reviewer subagent, ‚Č§3 iterations,
     fix/interview per issue),
     (3) present the reviewed SPEC for approval, (4) implement per SPEC. Do NOT
     start implementing
     before SPEC approval.

     Binding interview decisions

     - Clean rename check‚Üísite_pre (no alias); unknown bare phase names = loud
     fatal error.
     - site_post_dns fires right after custom_domains/primary_domain are
     computed (~line¬†1700),
     BEFORE site_url/WP-network detection and the existing DNS notice blocks.
     - [Cloudflare.cachecheck].enabled defaults false (opt-in); missing
     account_id/list_name
     while enabled = fatal.
     - Egress check verifies both IP families (family skipped if no
     connectivity; fatal if no
     family yields an IP, or any obtained IP is off-list).
     - Redirects: per-URL chain, max 5 same-FQDN hops.
     - RNG seeded from {site_name}:{report_date} (reproducible reruns, monthly
     rotation).
     - Full GET bodies, no size caps.
     - Test strategy: integration tests via one monkeypatchable HTTP seam +
     syrupy snapshot of notice
     HTML through the real template path; no new golden (all 3 goldens have
     Cloudflare disabled).
     - MISS-retry expansion: on MISS with otherwise-cacheable headers (‚Č•3-day
     cache time, no
     disqualifying directives): sleep 2s ‚Üí refetch ‚Üí still MISS ‚Üí sleep 2s ‚Üí
     third fetch ‚Üí still
     MISS ‚Üí result item. EXPIRED/STALE/etc. never retry.
     - Expansions IN scope: relocate umich fqdns-gated WP/Drush checks to
     check/umich at
     site_post_gather; recursive gate_disabled_sections; U-M doc suggestions
     incl. drafting a
     new "Understanding your Cloudflare cache report" page (SPEC content, user
     publishes manually).
     - NOT in scope: results persistence (DB), diagnostic-only CLI mode,
     http‚Üíhttps probe (future
     security-scoring work), MISS‚ÜíHIT beyond the retry protocol above.

     MUST early-return on create_tables (also update, import_older_metrics,

     Design

     1. Recursive gate_disabled_sections (land first, independent)

     Recurse into nested dict values: nested enabled is False table ‚Üí
     {'enabled': False};
     disabled parent still drops children entirely; "false" strings/missing/True
     untouched.
     Update docstring + tests/unit/test_section_gating.py (nested-disabled,
     disabled-parent-wins,
     enabled-child-with-disabled-grandchild, string-"false"-at-depth cases).

     2. Named ordered phases

     script_context.py: add
     PHASES = ('setup', 'site_pre', 'site_post_traffic', 'site_post_dns', 
     'site_post_gather', 'site_pre_render');
     hooks = {p: [] for p in PHASES}; add_hook/invoke_hooks validate: bare name
     must be in
     PHASES (else red error + sys.exit(1)); dotted names (contain .) remain
     plugin-defined events.
     Document phases + contract in the PHASES docstring/comment. Within-phase
     order stays
     module-name-deterministic (find_modules sorts; insertion order preserved).

     Main-script insertion points (all site hooks receive exactly
     (site_context)):

     4. check/cloudflare/ package

     __init__.py   gate: [Cloudflare].enabled AND
     [Cloudflare.cachecheck].enabled; deferred imports
                   in try/except ImportError ‚Üí clear message naming missing
     package +
                   "uv pip install .[cloudflare]"; validate config; register
     egress‚Üísetup,
                   cache‚Üísite_post_dns; else yellow skip message (house style)
     cfg.py        defaults + validation (fatal listing missing of
     account_id/list_name)
     httpseam.py   FetchResult dataclass; fetch()/sleep module attrs = THE
     monkeypatch seams
     headers.py    PURE per-URL header battery
     pages.py      PURE link/asset extraction + RNG selection +
     classify_redirect
     notices.py    PURE item‚ÜíHTML (U-M/generic variants) + cross-FQDN
     consolidation
     egress.py     setup-phase egress-IP allowlist check
     cache.py      site_post_dns orchestration + console output (make_rng module
     attr)

     Config [Cloudflare.cachecheck]: enabled=false, account_id, list_name,
     user_agent
     (default pantheon-sitehealth-emails (Linux; UMich WWS 0.1) 
     webmaster@umich.edu), timeout=5,
     report_doc_url (placeholder for the future U-M consolidated page;
     config-overridable). U-M
     values (b6a4063d6fa89fba31cf8bf99540d7e5 / um_networks) go in the private
     live config;
     sample toml documents everything.

     CLI: --allow-any-source-ip (store_true, model --only-warn :194-199).

     Deps: cloudflare = ["cloudflare", "httpx", "beautifulsoup4"] extra; add
     httpx+bs4 to the
     test extra too.

     egress.py: early-return on update/import_older_metrics/create_tables/
     allow_any_source_ip (create-tables return is REQUIRED ‚ÄĒ setup hooks run on
     that path).
     Per-family IP discovery (probe module attr = seam):
     https://1.1.1.1/cdn-cgi/trace /
     https://[2606:4700:4700::1111]/cdn-cgi/trace (parse ip=), fallback
     https://ip-check-perf.radar.cloudflare.com/ (JSON ip_address), fallback
     https://ifconfig.me/ (bare IP) ‚ÄĒ hostname fallbacks force family via
     httpx.HTTPTransport(local_address='0.0.0.0'|'::'). Family with all probes
     dead ‚Üí console note,
     skipped; no family with an IP ‚Üí fatal. Allowlist via
     sc.plugin_context['plugin.cloudflare']['get_client']() (shared client,
     house rule) ‚Üí
     client.rules.lists.list(account_id=‚Ä¶) name‚Üíid (missing list ‚Üí fatal) ‚Üí
     client.rules.lists.items.list(‚Ä¶) ‚Üí ipaddress.ip_network(item.ip, 
     strict=False); membership
     per family; off-list IP ‚Üí fatal naming the IP, list, and
     --allow-any-source-ip override.

     headers.py (pure): parse_cache_control (tolerant, never raises),
     cache_seconds
     (max of max-age/s-maxage, None if neither), evaluate_headers(headers, 
     is_main_page, now, http_status) -> list[Item], should_retry_miss(headers, 
     items). Item ids (= consolidation
     identity): cf-status-missing, cf-status-uncacheable, no-cache-control,
     no-max-age,
     short-cache-time, cc-private, cc-no-cache, cc-no-store,
     cc-proxy-revalidate,
     cc-must-revalidate (non-main-page only; main page OK ‚ÄĒ emergency-alert
     convention),
     expires-short (only when CC absent-or-lacking max-age/s-maxage),
     set-cookie,
     set-cookie-bypass (REPLACES the BYPASS uncacheable item when Set-Cookie
     present),
     http-error, plus transport items timeout, invalid-cert, challenge,
     request-failed,
     and miss-persistent. Constants: acceptable statuses {HIT, MISS, EXPIRED,
     STALE, REVALIDATED,
     UPDATING}; 3-day floor; 31536000 recommendation; 2s retry delay.

     pages.py (pure): extract_page_links (bs4; https same-FQDN/relative only;
     exclude
     main-page+fragments and the PROMPT's auth/API prefixes; dedupe; sort),
     choose_pages (‚Č§3 via
     rng), extract_assets (script src/link rel=stylesheet href/img src ‚Üí
     js/css/img lists),
     choose_assets (‚Č§1 per class), classify_redirect(current, location, fqdn) ->
     'follow'|'cross'
     (http‚Üíhttps same-URL upgrade and same-FQDN follow; apex‚ÜĒwww is 'cross').

     httpseam.py: fresh httpx.Client(follow_redirects=False, trust_env=False, 
     verify=‚Ä¶, timeout=cfg, headers={'user-agent': cfg}) per fetch (no cookies
     sent); manual redirect loop,
     max 5 same-FQDN hops; cross-FQDN ‚Üí error='cross_fqdn_redirect' (console
     note, drop URL, NO
     item); cf-mitigated: challenge ‚Üí error='challenge'; SSL error ‚Üí
     error='cert' (caller adds
     item, refetches verify=False, continues battery on that response);
     timeout/conn errors ‚Üí
     respective error values. Full body read.

     cache.py: skip unless fqdns_behind_cloudflare; rng = make_rng(site, 
     report_date);
     sequential per sorted FQDN: main page ‚Üí battery(is_main_page=True) ‚Üí links
     ‚Üí ‚Č§3 chosen pages ‚Üí
     for each requested page (main included): battery + asset selection (‚Č§1
     js/css/img) + battery per
     asset. MISS-retry protocol per binding decision. Console: verbosity 0 ‚Üí
     sc.console.status
     updated per FQDN/step (ephemeral); -v ‚Üí non-ephemeral step lines; -vvv ‚Üí
     full request line +
     status + all response headers via sc.debug(level=3); result items ‚Üí
     immediate
     sc.console.print ALWAYS (concise technical wording, URL + page-vs-asset +
     test + problem).

     notices.py: item key = (id, sorted(params)) excluding URL; per-FQDN
     signature =
     frozenset of keys; group FQDNs by signature ‚Üí ONE warning notice per group
     ("Cloudflare
     caching", all group FQDNs + tested URLs listed). csv:
     {site},cloudflare-cache,‚Ä¶ for ALL
     notices from this check. Two language variants per item selected by U-M
     gating (config-based
     check, importable standalone): U-M ‚Üí documentation.its.umich.edu links
     (respecting the verified
     anchor inventory + report_doc_url); generic ‚Üí
     Pantheon/Cloudflare/MDN/Wikipedia. House
     escaping only (sc.escape_url + html.escape); never suggest
     disabling/bypassing caching.

‚óŹ¬†User answered Claude's questions:
  ‚éŅ ¬†¬∑ The reviewer caught that the spec (echoing PROMPT's sketch 'site_pre 
     (site_context created)') mislabels where site_pre actually fires. The 
     SiteContext is created at ~:1404, but today's 'check' seam is at :1598 ‚ÄĒ 
     after plan validation, env:list, the traffic gather/DB merge, and 
     (critically) after the --update/--import-older-metrics continues. Moving 
     the invocation to :1404 would match the PROMPT sketch but changes behavior:
     site_pre hooks (SiteLens today) would start firing during --update and 
     --import-older-metrics runs, which they never did. Keeping it at :1598 
     preserves behavior exactly but the phase must be honestly documented as 
     'first per-site seam, adjacent to site_post_traffic' rather than 'right 
     after creation'. ‚Üí Keep at :1598 (Recommended)
     ¬∑ ¬ß12's CMS-link note claimed framework info isn't available at 
     site_post_dns ‚ÄĒ the reviewer proved that false: 
     site_context['site']['framework'] comes from the Pantheon site record and 
     is available from the start. So the U-M notice variants CAN link 
     CMS-appropriate install docs (WordPress ‚Üí node/5114, Drupal ‚Üí node/4242) 
     where relevant (e.g. no-cache-control, set-cookie items). Alternative: keep
     notices CMS-neutral (doc_url/node/4241/node/5110 only) and leave 
     CMS-install nudges entirely to the relocated check/umich/cloudflare_cms.py 
     check. ‚Üí CMS-appropriate links (Recommended)
     ¬∑ PROMPT redirect rule: same-FQDN redirects are re-requested 'a maximum of 
     5 times', and 'for everything else, note it in the console output and move 
     on ‚ÄĒ do not add a result item'. What happens when the 5-hop budget is 
     exhausted is genuinely ambiguous: 'everything else' plainly covers 
     cross-FQDN targets, but a 6th same-FQDN redirect (likely a redirect loop) 
     isn't clearly assigned. The spec currently adds a too-many-redirects result
     item (a loop is a real, owner-visible problem); the strict reading treats 
     exhaustion like 'everything else' ‚ÄĒ console note only, no item. ‚Üí Result 
     item (Recommended)

       34 +                                                              
       35 +TRACE_URLS = {                                                
       36 +    4: "https://1.1.1.1/cdn-cgi/trace",                       
       37 +    6: "https://[2606:4700:4700::1111]/cdn-cgi/trace",        
       38 +}                                                             
       39 +FALLBACK_RADAR = "https://ip-check-perf.radar.cloudflare.com/"
          +  # JSON: ip_address                                          
       40 +# The bare / path of ifconfig.me content-negotiates on User-Ag
          +ent and can return HTML;                                      
       41 +# /ip always returns the bare address:                        
       42 +FALLBACK_IFCONFIG = "https://ifconfig.me/ip"                  
       43 +LOCAL_ADDR = {4: "0.0.0.0", 6: "::"}                          
       44 +

       46 +def _parse_trace(text: str):  # -> str | None                 
       47 +    for line in text.splitlines():                            
       48 +        if line.startswith("ip="):                            
       49 +            return line[3:].strip()                           
       50 +    return None                                               
       51 +                                                              
       52 +                                                              
       53 +def _parse_radar(text: str):  # -> str | None                 
       54 +    try:                                                      
       55 +        data = json.loads(text)                               
       56 +    except ValueError:                                        
       57 +        return None                                           
       58 +    return data.get("ip_address") if isinstance(data, dict) el
          +se None                                                       
       59 +                                                              
       60 +                                                              
       61 +def _parse_ifconfig(text: str):  # -> str | None              
       62 +    return text.strip() or None                               
       63 +                                                              
       64 +                                                              
       65 +_ENDPOINTS = {                                                
       66 +    family: (                                                 
       67 +        (TRACE_URLS[family], _parse_trace),                   
       68 +        (FALLBACK_RADAR, _parse_radar),                       
       69 +        (FALLBACK_IFCONFIG, _parse_ifconfig),                 
       70 +    )                                                         
       71 +    for family in (4, 6)                                      
       72 +}                                                             
       73 +                                                              
       74 +                                                              
       75 +def _probe(url: str, family: int, timeout: float, user_agent: 
          +str):  # -> str | None                                        
       76 +    """GET one probe endpoint over the given IP family; body t
          +ext, or None on any                                           
       77 +    failure (connection-level failures cascade to the next end
          +point)."""                                                    
       78 +    try:                                                      
       79 +        transport = httpx.HTTPTransport(local_address=LOCAL_AD
          +DR[family])                                                   
       80 +        with httpx.Client(transport=transport, timeout=timeout
          +, trust_env=False,                                            
       81 +                          headers={"user-agent": user_agent}) 
          +as client:                                                    
       82 +            response = client.get(url)                        
       83 +    except httpx.HTTPError:                                   
       84 +        return None                                           
       85 +    except OSError:  # e.g. no IPv6 support at the socket leve
          +l                                                             
       86 +        return None                                           
       87 +    if response.status_code != 200:                           
       88 +        return None                                           
       89 +    return response.text                                      
       90 +                                                              
       91 +                                                              
       92 +probe = _probe  # module attribute = the egress-check monkeypa
          +tch seam                                                      
       93 +                                                              
       94 +                                                              
       95 +def _discover_ip(family: int, timeout: float, user_agent: str)
          +:  # -> str | None                                            
       96 +    """This host's external IPv4/IPv6 address via the probe ch
          +ain; None when the family                                     
       97 +    has no working endpoint at all (= no connectivity, skipped
          + by the caller)."""                                           
       98 +    for url, parser in _ENDPOINTS[family]:                    
       99 +        text = probe(url, family, timeout, user_agent)        
      100 +        if text is None:                                      
      101 +            continue                                          
      102 +        ip = parser(text)                                     
      103 +        if ip is None:                                        
      104 +            sc.debug(f"Egress probe {url} returned no usable I
          +Pv{family} address", level=2)                                 
      105 +            continue                                          
      106 +        try:                                                  
      107 +            address = ipaddress.ip_address(ip.strip())        
      108 +        except ValueError:                                    
      109 +            sc.debug(f"Egress probe {url} returned unparseable
          + address {ip!r}", level=2)                                    
      110 +            continue                                          
      111 +        if address.version != family:                         
      112 +            # A mismatched-family answer counts as probe failu
          +re (the backstop for the                                      
      113 +            # local_address family-pinning caveat in the modul
          +e docstring):                                                 
      114 +            sc.debug(f"Egress probe {url} answered with an IPv
          +{address.version} address "                                   
      115 +                     f"while probing IPv{family}; ignoring", l
          +evel=2)                                                       
      116 +            continue                                          
      117 +        sc.debug(f"Egress IPv{family} address {address} (via {
          +url})")                                                       
      118 +        return str(address)                                   
      119 +    return None                                               
      120 +                                                              
      121 +                                                              
      122 +def _fetch_allowlist(cfg: dict) -> list:                      
      123 +    """The configured Cloudflare list's entries as ip_network 
          +objects.  Any API error,                                      
      124 +    a missing list, or a list with no IP entries is fatal.""" 
      125 +    account_id = cfg["account_id"]                            
      126 +    list_name = cfg["list_name"]                              
      127 +    client = sc.plugin_context["plugin.cloudflare"]["get_clien
          +t"]()

          +t_id))                                                        
      130 +    except cloudflare.CloudflareError as e:

          + for account {account_id}: "                                  
      132 +                 f"{e}  (the credentials may lack the \"Accoun
          +t Filter Lists: Read\" scope)")                               
      133 +    matches = [l for l in lists if getattr(l, "name", None) ==
          + list_name]                                                   
      134 +    if not matches:                                           
      135 +        sys.exit(f"ERROR: Cloudflare list '{list_name}' was no
          +t found in account "                                          
      136 +                 f"{account_id}.  Check [Cloudflare.cachecheck
          +].list_name and the "                                         
      137 +                 f"credentials' \"Account Filter Lists: Read\"
          + scope.")

          +account_id,                                                   
      140 +                                                   list_id=mat
          +ches[0].id))                                                  
      141 +    except cloudflare.CloudflareError as e:                   
      142 +        sys.exit(f"ERROR: unable to fetch the items of Cloudfl
          +are list '{list_name}' "                                      
      143 +                 f"(account {account_id}): {e}")              
      144 +    networks = []                                             
      145 +    for item in items:                                        
      146 +        ip = getattr(item, "ip", None)                        
      147 +        if not ip:                                            
      148 +            sc.console.print(f"[yellow]Ignoring a non-IP entry
          + in Cloudflare list "                                         
      149 +                             f"'{list_name}' (only IP lists ma
          +ke sense here)")                                              
      150 +            continue                                          
      151 +        try:                                                  
      152 +            networks.append(ipaddress.ip_network(ip, strict=Fa
          +lse))                                                         
      153 +        except ValueError:                                    
      154 +            sc.console.print(f"[yellow]Ignoring unparseable en
          +try {ip!r} in Cloudflare "                                    
      155 +                             f"list '{list_name}'")           
      156 +    if not networks:                                          
      157 +        sys.exit(f"ERROR: Cloudflare list '{list_name}' (accou
          +nt {account_id}) contains "                                   
      158 +                 f"no IP entries; the egress-IP check can neve
          +r pass.  Populate the list "                                  
      159 +                 f"or run with --allow-any-source-ip.")       
      160 +    return networks                                           
      161 +                                                              
      162 +                                                              
      163 +def check_egress_ip() -> None:                                
      164 +    """The setup hook.  Fatal unless every IP family with conn
          +ectivity egresses from an                                     
      165 +    address on the configured allowlist."""                   
      166 +    options = sc.options                                      
      167 +    if (options.update or options.import_older_metrics or opti
          +ons.create_tables                                             
      168 +            or options.allow_any_source_ip):                  
      169 +        sc.debug("Skipping the egress-IP allowlist check (not 
          +a report run, or "                                            
      170 +                 "--allow-any-source-ip was given)")          
      171 +        return                                                
      172 +    cfg = cachecheck_config()                                 
      173 +    with sc.console.status("[bold green]Verifying this host's 
          +egress IP addresses "                                         
      174 +                           "against the Cloudflare allowlist")
          +:                                                             
      175 +        ips = {}                                              
      176 +        for family in (4, 6):                                 
      177 +            ips[family] = _discover_ip(family, cfg["timeout"],
          + cfg["user_agent"])                                           
      178 +            if ips[family] is None:                           
      179 +                sc.console.print(f"[yellow]No IPv{family} conn
          +ectivity detected; "                                          
      180 +                                 f"skipping the IPv{family} eg
          +ress check")                                                  
      181 +        if not any(ips.values()):                             
      182 +            sys.exit("ERROR: could not determine this host's e
          +xternal IP address "                                          
      183 +                     "(all probe endpoints failed for both IPv
          +4 and IPv6)")                                                 
      184 +        networks = _fetch_allowlist(cfg)                      
      185 +        for family, ip in ips.items():                        
      186 +            if ip is None:                                    
      187 +                continue                                      
      188 +            address = ipaddress.ip_address(ip)                
      189 +            if not any(address in net for net in networks if n
          +et.version == family):                                        
      190 +                sys.exit(f"ERROR: this host's IPv{family} egre
          +ss address {ip} is not in "                                   
      191 +                         f"Cloudflare list '{cfg['list_name']}
          +' (account "                                                  
      192 +                         f"{cfg['account_id']}).  Cache checks
          + from here would see "                                        
      193 +                         f"challenge/external behavior.  Run f
          +rom an allow-listed "                                         
      194 +                         f"network, add this address to the li
          +st, or pass "                                                 
      195 +                         f"--allow-any-source-ip.")           
      196 +    sc.console.print("Egress IP allowlist check passed: "     
      197 +                     + ", ".join(f"IPv{family} {ip}"          
      198 +                                 for family, ip in ips.items()
          + if ip))

          +lt.status_code < 300)

      156 +def _check_fqdn(fqdn: str, cfg: dict, rng, status) -> list:

‚óŹ Update(CLAUDE.md)
  ‚éŅ ¬†Added 11 lines, removed 3 lines
      83  `<{secret env NAME}` substitutions, with an optional trailing d
          efault) registers
      84  **unconditionally** ‚ÄĒ no `[Env]` section ‚ÄĒ because it has no de
          pendency and core config
      85  (`[SMTP].username = "<{env USER}"`) needs it. Modules register 
          by:
      86 -- **Hooks** ‚ÄĒ `sc.add_hook('setup', {...})` or appending to `sc
         -.hooks['check']`. `setup`                                      
      87 -  hooks run once (DB connections, fetching Cloudflare IPs, etc.
         -); `check` hooks run once                                      
      88 -  per site with the site's `site_context`. Invoked via `sc.invo
         -ke_hooks(name, ...)`.                                          
      86 +- **Hooks** ‚ÄĒ `sc.add_hook('<phase>', {'name': ‚Ä¶, 'func': ‚Ä¶})`.
         + Phases are the ordered                                        
      87 +  `sc.PHASES` tuple: `setup` (once per run ‚ÄĒ **including `--cre
         +ate-tables`**, which exits                                     
      88 +  later), then per site `site_pre` (rename of the old `check` s
         +eam), `site_post_traffic`,                                     
      89 +  `site_post_dns`, `site_post_gather`, `site_pre_render`. Each 
         +site phase receives the                                        
      90 +  `SiteContext`; the per-phase guaranteed keys are the data-con
         +tract table below. Bare                                        
      91 +  names not in `PHASES` are a **fatal error** in both `add_hook
         +` and `invoke_hooks`;                                          
      92 +  dotted names (e.g. `setup.umich.portal`) are plugin-defined e
         +vents, allowed and                                             
      93 +  invoked by whoever owns them. Gating: phases through `site_po
         +st_gather` run on                                              
      94 +  full-report and `--only-warn` paths; `site_pre_render` full-r
         +eport only; `--update`/                                        
      95 +  `--import-older-metrics` never reach any site phase; a per-si
         +te fatal error (e.g.                                           
      96 +  domain:list failure) skips that site's remaining phases.

  The process worked as intended on my own code: the top finding (drupal_modules
  stuffed with an isinstance(list) check when drush pm:list returns a dict) is
  a real regression I introduced in the relocation ‚ÄĒ it silently kills the four
  relocated Drupal checks in production and was masked by a test fixture with
  the same wrong shape. Findings 2‚Äď4 are run-killers reachable from remote page
  content or a plausible config (InvalidURL escape, rich MarkupError at -v, the
  News √ó recursive-gating startup fatal).

  Notable refutations (with citations): the max(max-age, s-maxage) semantics and
  the U-M default user-agent are verbatim PROMPT requirements; the
  notice-ordering shift was recorded as accepted in SPEC ¬ß7; full-GET-no-caps
  was your explicit interview choice. Two of those are worth an upstream thought
  sometime: Cloudflare's edge actually honors s-maxage over max-age, so
  max-age=31536000, s-maxage=0 passes the battery today.

  Cut by the 10-cap (all verified PLAUSIBLE/CONFIRMED, lower severity): the
  module-loader idiom duplicated 9 more times across new test files, doc-URL
  constants in two homes, _a() bypassed in notice assembly, _MISS_RETRY_BLOCKERS
  hand-sync drift (4 of 10 members provably dead), the items out-param flow,
  double HTML parse of the main page, sequential egress probes, dotted-hook-name
  typos being silent no-ops, and no code enforcement of the phase key contract.

  regression + the crash paths + the two doc/diagnostic corrections) ‚ÄĒ all
  small, test-covered changes.

‚óŹ All 10 findings fixed, verified, and live-smoked. Summary:

  1. drupal_modules dict bug ‚ÄĒ stuffing now isinstance(mods, dict); test
  fixtures corrected to the real dict shape, plus a new regression test that
  runs the real sc.check_drupal_module end-to-end (a list-shaped fixture would
  now fail it, closing the masking hole).
  2. httpx.InvalidURL escape ‚ÄĒ named catch in httpseam._fetch ‚Üí
  error='connection' with detail; new tests/integration/test_httpseam.py proves
  control-byte and 70k-char URLs are contained offline.
  3. rich MarkupError ‚ÄĒ every debug path embedding remote strings (_step,
  _debug_response, link/asset/retry lines) now rich_escapes; new test runs the
  check at -vvv with a [/red] URL.
  4. News √ó recursive gating ‚ÄĒ load_news_items skips items with enabled is False
  (both config-inline and file-based, with an isinstance guard for scalars);
  three new tests including the stripped-{'enabled': False} shape.
  5. Duplicate URLs in notices ‚ÄĒ url_lines dedupes by URL (requests stay
  un-deduped per the PROMPT); new consolidation test.
  6. _transport_item KeyError ‚ÄĒ .get(..., "request-failed") fallback with the
  raw error as reason; new test drives the double-cert path.
  7. Contract doc ‚ÄĒ CLAUDE.md table row and the stuffing comment now state
  "unknown"/"" semantics for the version/url keys and the dict shape for
  drupal_modules.
  8. ImportError over-catch ‚ÄĒ internal package ImportErrors (e.name starting
  with the package name) re-raise with the real traceback; new test asserts a
  typo'd .cfg import raises instead of printing the install hint.
  9. Path over-exclusion ‚ÄĒ bare markers now match on segment boundaries only
  (exact, +"/", +"."), so /wp-login.php and /login/reset are still excluded but
  /registered-programs, /profiles, /tokens are probed; exclusion tests rewritten
  with both directions.
  10. Per-URL TLS handshakes ‚ÄĒ new httpseam.ClientPool (per-FQDN, lazy
  verify=False client, cookie jar cleared before every request ‚ÄĒ which also
  fixed a latent within-redirect-chain cookie replay); threaded through
  _check_fqdn/_test_url/_run_miss_retries.

  Verification: full ./run-tests 403 passed (was 378; +25 tests), all 10
  snapshots pass, e2e goldens byte-identical. Live smoke against
  accreditation.umich.edu through the new ClientPool path returns the identical
  22 findings as before the change (determinism intact).

  Two notes for the record: fix #9 deviates from SPEC ¬ß8.7's literal
  prefix-of-path wording (the SPEC file is unedited ‚ÄĒ it's the historical
  record; docs//code comments carry the new semantics), and fix #10 supersedes
  SPEC ¬ß8.5's "fresh client per fetch" wording (the PROMPT's actual rule ‚ÄĒ never
  send cookies ‚ÄĒ is preserved and now enforced per-hop too).
